   function convertToEntities(tstr)
    {
      var bstr = '';
      for(i = 0; i &lt; tstr.length; ++i)
        {
          if(tstr.charCodeAt(i) &gt; 127)
        {
          bstr += '&amp;#' + tstr.charCodeAt(i) + ';';
        }
      else
        {
          bstr += tstr.charAt(i);
        }
        }
      return bstr;
    }

  function checkReplacementChr(tstr) {
    if (encodeURI(tstr).indexOf("%EF%BF%BD") &gt;= 0) {
      return false;
    } else {
      return true;
    }
  }

      <script type="text/javascript">
       if (typeof alphabet === "undefined") {
   if (typeof String.prototype.startsWith != 'function') {
     // see below for better implementation!
     String.prototype.startsWith = function (str){
       return this.indexOf(str) == 0;
     };
   }

   // var alphabet = { "english" : "abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz" };

   var alphabet = {
      "initiated" : 0,
      "lookfor" : {
         "reset" : function () {
            if (alphabet.lookfor.timestamp.getTime() &lt; new Date().getTime()) {
               alphabet.lookfor.string = "";
               return true;
            }
            alphabet.lookin = [];
            alphabet.lookinState = -1;
            // console.log ( alphabet.lookfor.timestamp,  new Date(), alphabet.lookfor.string) ;
            return false;
         },
         "timestamp" : new Date(),
         "string" : "",
         "element" : []
      },
      "lookin" : [],
      "lookinState" : -1,
      "init" : function (element) {
         var lang = "english";
         this.generate (lang);
          jQuery(element).each(function(index){
            alphabet.lookfor.element[alphabet.lookfor.element.length] = 30*index+4;
         });
        this.initiated = 1;
      },
      "generate" : function (lang) {
         for (var cc = this[lang].charCodeRange.start; cc &lt;= this[lang].charCodeRange.end; cc++) {
            this[lang].string += String.fromCharCode(cc).toLowerCase();
         } // END FOR
         return true;
      },
      "gotoString" : function () {
         alphabet.lookinState = alphabet.lookinState + 1;
         if (typeof alphabet.lookin[alphabet.lookinState] === "undefined") {
            alphabet.lookinState = 0;
         }
         var scrollto = alphabet.lookfor.element[alphabet.lookin[alphabet.lookinState]];
         jQuery('#member-area #location .dropdown-menu').animate({
           scrollTop: scrollto
         }, 0);
         jQuery('#location &gt; ul &gt; li &gt; a').removeClass('hover');
         jQuery(jQuery('#location &gt; ul &gt; li &gt; a')[alphabet.lookin[alphabet.lookinState]]).addClass('hover');
         setTimeout (function(){jQuery('#location &gt; ul &gt; li &gt; a').removeClass('hover');},2000);
         return true;
      },
      "english" : {
         "charCodeRange" : {
            "start": 65,
            "end": 90
         },
         "string" : ""
      }
   };

   alphabet.init('#location &gt; ul &gt; li &gt; a');

}

jQuery(document).keypress(function(event){

   if (jQuery('#location.open').length &gt; 0) {
      var keyCode = event.keyCode || event.which;

      if (keyCode !== 9) {

         var keypressed = String.fromCharCode(keyCode).toLowerCase();
         alphabet.lookfor.reset();

         if (alphabet['english'].string.startsWith(keypressed) &gt;= 0) {
            alphabet.lookfor.string += keypressed;
            alphabet.lookfor.timestamp = new Date();
            alphabet.lookfor.timestamp.setSeconds(alphabet.lookfor.timestamp.getSeconds() + 1);
         }

         jQuery('#location &gt; ul &gt; li &gt; a').each(function(index){
            if (jQuery.trim(jQuery(this).text()).toLowerCase().startsWith(alphabet.lookfor.string.toLowerCase()) ) {
               alphabet.lookin[alphabet.lookin.length] = index;
            }
         });
      }
      if (alphabet.lookin.length &gt; 0){
         alphabet.gotoString();
      }
   }

});
      </script>

     <script>
      var switch_bg = "";

          jQuery(document).ready(function() {

            jQuery("#megamenu").mouseleave(function() {
              showmm("clear");
            });


            jQuery('#header').mouseleave(function(){
              showmm("clear");
            });


            jQuery("ul#categories li").each(function(index){
              jQuery(this).hover(function(){
                megaMenuTimer = setTimeout(function(){
                  showmm('mm'+(index+1));
                  ajxmegamenu('http://www.hobbyking.com/hobbyking/store/customerScoring.asp?type='+(index+1))
                },300);
              },function(){
                clearTimeout(megaMenuTimer);
              })
            });


          });


          function showmm(mmvar) {
            jQuery("#megamenu .links").hide();
            if (mmvar != "clear") {
              jQuery("#megamenu").show();
              jQuery('#'+mmvar).show();
            } else {
              jQuery("#megamenu").hide();
            }
          }

          function ajxmegamenu(pagevar,destinationvar) {
            jQuery.ajax({
              url:pagevar
            });
          }
     </script>

    ================================================== -->
     <script>
      $(function()
	{
		//alert("['Fabrikator 3D Printer', 'TALI FPV Hexacopter', 'Brushless Gimbal', 'TrackStar ROAR Approved', 'EFX Racer', 'RTF Quad', 'Quanum Venture FPV', 'DJI products', 'Assault Reaper 3D Quad', 'Tri-pod For FPV Monitors and Cameras']");
		var default_value = "Fabrikator 3D Printer";
		var placeholder = "Fabrikator 3D Printer";
		
		var keyword_source = ['Fabrikator 3D Printer', 'TALI FPV Hexacopter', 'Brushless Gimbal', 'TrackStar ROAR Approved', 'EFX Racer', 'RTF Quad', 'Quanum Venture FPV', 'DJI products', 'Assault Reaper 3D Quad', 'Tri-pod For FPV Monitors and Cameras'];
		var url_source = ['//www.hobbyking.com/hobbyking/store/RC_PRODUCT_SEARCH.asp?strSearch=Fabrikator%203D%20Printer', '//www.hobbyking.com/hobbyking/store/RC_PRODUCT_SEARCH.asp?strSearch=Walkera%20TALI%20H500', '//www.hobbyking.com/hobbyking/store/__963__960__Multi_Rotors_Parts-Brushless_Gimbals.html', '//www.hobbyking.com/hobbyking/store/RC_PRODUCT_SEARCH.asp?strSearch=TrackStar%20Roar%20Approved', '//www.hobbyking.com/hobbyking/store/RC_PRODUCT_SEARCH.asp?strSearch=EFX%20Racer%20Model', '//www.hobbyking.com/hobbyking/store/__592__501__Multi_Rotors_Parts-RTF_PNF_ARF.html', '//www.hobbyking.com/hobbyking/store/RC_PRODUCT_SEARCH.asp?strSearch=Quanum%20Venture%20FPV', '//www.hobbyking.com/hobbyking/store/__1260__501__Multi_Rotors_Parts-DJI_Products.html', '//www.hobbyking.com/hobbyking/store/RC_PRODUCT_SEARCH.asp?strSearch=Assault%20Reaper%203D%20Quad', '//www.hobbyking.com/hobbyking/store/RC_PRODUCT_SEARCH.asp?strSearch=Lightweight%20Aluminum%20Tripod'];
		
		var keyword_url_mapping = {};
		
		for(i=0;i&lt;keyword_source.length;i++)
		{
			keyword_url_mapping[keyword_source[i]] = url_source[i];
		}
		//alert($("input[name='strSearch']").attr('name'));
		var new_suggestion = $("input[name='strSearch']").autocomplete({
			source: keyword_source,
			minLength: 0,
			select: function(event, ui)
			{
				var go_to = keyword_url_mapping[ui.item.value];
				//alert(go_to);
				location.href = go_to;
			},
			focus: function(event, ui)
			{
				var selectedObj = ui.item;              
				$(ui.item).css({"font-size":"100px!important"});
			}
		});
		
		$( "#ui-id-1" ).css({background:"none",backgroundColor:"rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.6)"});

		$("input[name='strSearch']").click(function()
		{
			var c_value = $.trim($(this).val());
			//var c_value = $.trim(this.value);
			
			//var type = $(".dropdown-menu").find("[aria-labelledby='search-product-list']").attr("class");
			if(($.inArray(c_value, keyword_source)!=-1) || (c_value==""))
			{
				if($("#search_result_menu").css("display") == "block")
				{
					$(this).autocomplete("disable");
				}
				else
				{
					$(this).val("");
					$(this).autocomplete("enable");
				}
			}
			else if(c_value != "")
			{
				$(this).autocomplete("disable");
			}

			$(this).attr("placeholder","");
			$(this).autocomplete("search", "");
			
			$(".ui-corner-all").css({'color':"white",
									 'font-size':"14px"
									});
			$(".ui-state-focus").css({'backgroundColor':"rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.8)"});
		});
		
		$("input[name='strSearch']").focusout(function()
		{
			var c_value = $.trim($(this).val());
			if(c_value=="")
			{	
				$(this).autocomplete("enable");
				//this.value = default_value;
				$(this).val(default_value);
			}
			$(this).attr("placeholder", placeholder);
		});

		$("input[name='strSearch']").keypress(function()
		{
			$(this).autocomplete("disable");
		});
	});
     </script>

          <script language="javascript">
           function openYoutube2(id, videoType){
      window.scrollTo(0, 0);

      //YouTube Player Parameters
      var width = 640;
      var height = 505;
      var FullScreen = "yes";
      var AutoPlay = "yes";
      var HighDef = "yes";

      //Calculate Page width and height
      var pageWidth = window.innerWidth;
      var pageHeight = window.innerHeight;
      if (typeof pageWidth != "number"){
      if (document.compatMode == "CSS1Compat"){
        pageWidth = document.documentElement.clientWidth;
        pageHeight = document.documentElement.clientHeight;
      } else {
        pageWidth = document.body.clientWidth;
        pageHeight = document.body.clientHeight;
        }
      }
      // Make Background visible...
      var divbg = document.getElementById('bg');
      divbg.style.visibility = "visible";

      //Create dynamic Div container for YouTube Popup Div
      var divobj = document.createElement('div');
      divobj.setAttribute('id',id); // Set id to YouTube id
      divobj.className = "popup";
      divobj.style.visibility = "visible";
      divobj.style.zIndex = 999;
      divobj.style.position = "absolute";

      var divWidth = width + 4;
      var divHeight = height + 20;
      divobj.style.width = divWidth + "px";
      divobj.style.height = divHeight + "px";
      var divLeft = (pageWidth - divWidth) / 2;
      var divTop = (pageHeight - divHeight) / 2 - 10;
      //Set Left and top coordinates for the div tag
      divobj.style.left = divLeft + "px";
      divobj.style.top = divTop + "px";

      //Create dynamic Close Button Div
      var closebutton = document.createElement('div');
      closebutton.style.visibility = "visible";
      closebutton.style.zIndex = 999;
      closebutton.style.position = "relative";

      closebutton.innerHTML = "&lt;img align=\"right\" style=\"cursor:pointer;\" border=\"0\" src=\"images/close_bt.png\" onclick=\"closeYouTube('" + id +"')\" &gt;";
      //Add Close Button Div to YouTube Popup Div container
      divobj.appendChild(closebutton);

      //Create dynamic YouTube Div
      var ytobj = document.createElement('div');
      ytobj.setAttribute('id', "yt" + id);
      ytobj.className = "ytcontainer";
      ytobj.style.width = width + "px";
      ytobj.style.height = height + "px";
      //ytobj.style.z-index = 998;
      //ytobj.style.position = "relative";
      if (FullScreen == "yes") FullScreen="&amp;fs=1"; else FullScreen="&amp;fs=0";
      if (AutoPlay == "yes") AutoPlay="&amp;autoplay=1"; else AutoPlay="&amp;autoplay=0";
      if (HighDef == "yes") HighDef="&amp;hd=1"; else HighDef="&amp;hd=0";
      var URL = "http://www.youtube.com/v/" + id + "&amp;hl=en&amp;rel=0&amp;showsearch=0" + FullScreen + AutoPlay + HighDef;
      var YouTube = "&lt;object width=\"" + width + "\" height=\"" + height + "\"&gt;";

      YouTube += "&lt;param name=\"wmode\" value=\"transparent\"&gt;&lt;/param&gt;";

      YouTube += "&lt;param name=\"movie\" value=\"" + URL + "\"&gt;&lt;/param&gt;";
      YouTube += "&lt;param name=\"allowFullScreen\" value=\"true\"&gt;&lt;/param&gt;&lt;param name=\"allowscriptaccess\" value=\"always\"&gt;&lt;/param&gt;";
      YouTube += "&lt;embed src=\"" + URL + "\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\" ";
      YouTube += "allowscriptaccess=\"always\" allowfullscreen=\"true\" width=\"" + width + "\" height=\"" + height + "\"&gt;&lt;/embed&gt;&lt;/object&gt;";


      if (videoType == "Viddler") {

      YouTube = '&lt;!--[if IE]&gt;&lt;object width="'+ width +'" height="'+ height +'" id="viddlerOuter-'+ id +'" classid="clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000"&gt;&lt;param name="movie" value="//www.viddler.com/player/'+ id +'/"&gt;&lt;param name="allowScriptAccess" value="always"&gt;&lt;param name="allowNetworking" value="all"&gt;&lt;param name="allowFullScreen" value="true"&gt;&lt;param name="flashVars" value="f=1&amp;openURL=49636673&amp;autoplay=t&amp;title=&amp;hideablecontrolbar=1&amp;videobrowserfollowpermalink=1&amp;videobrowserfollowpermalinktarget=new&amp;loop=0&amp;nologo=0&amp;hd=0"&gt;&lt;obj'
       YouTube += 'ect id="viddlerInner-'+ id +'"&gt;&lt;video id="viddlerVideo-'+ id +'" src="//www.viddler.com/file/'+ id +'/html5mobile?openURL=49636673" type="video/mp4" width="'+ width +'" height="'+ height +'" poster="//www.viddler.com/thumbnail/'+ id +'/" controls="controls" x-webkit-airplay="allow"&gt;&lt;/video&gt;&lt;/object&gt;&lt;/object&gt;&lt;![endif]--&gt; &lt;!--[if !IE]&gt; &lt;!--&gt; &lt;object width="640" height="505" id="viddlerOuter-'+ id +'" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" data="//www.viddler.com/player/'+ id +'/"&gt; &lt;param name="movie" value="//www.viddler.com/player/'+ id +'/"&gt; &lt;param name="allowScriptAccess" value="always"&gt;&lt;param name="allowNetworking" value="all"&gt;&lt;param name="allowFullScreen" value="true"&gt;&lt;param name="flashVars" value="f=1&amp;openURL=49636673&amp;autoplay=t&amp;title=&amp;hideablecontrolbar=1&amp;videobrowserfollowpermalink=1&amp;videobrowserfollowpermalinktarget=new&amp;loop=0&amp;nologo=0&amp;hd=0"&gt;&lt;obj'
       YouTube += 'ect id="viddlerInner-'+ id +'"&gt; &lt;video id="viddlerVideo-'+ id +'" src="//www.viddler.com/file/'+ id +'/html5mobile?openURL=49636673" type="video/mp4" width="640" height="505" poster="//www.viddler.com/thumbnail/'+ id +'/" controls="controls" x-webkit-airplay="allow"&gt;&lt;/video&gt; &lt;/object&gt;&lt;/object&gt; &lt;!--&lt;![endif]--&gt;'

      }



      ytobj.innerHTML = YouTube;
      //Add YouTube Div to YouTube Popup Div container
      divobj.appendChild(ytobj);

      //Add YouTube Popup Div container to HTML BODY
      document.body.appendChild(divobj);
  }
  function closeYouTube(id){
      var divbg = document.getElementById('bg');
      divbg.style.visibility = "hidden";
      var divobj = document.getElementById(id);
      var ytobj = document.getElementById("yt" + id);
      divobj.removeChild(ytobj); //remove YouTube Div
      document.body.removeChild(divobj); // remove Popup Div
  }

              As the 3D Pen draws, it extrudes heated plastic, which quickly cools and solidifies into a strong stable structure. This allows you to build an infinite variety of shapes and items with ease! Even in mid airMost people will instantly be able to trace objects on paper, and after only a few hours of practice you will be able to make far more intricate objects.
             </p>
             <p class="MsoNormal">
              What can I make with a 3D Pen? Pretty much anything; there are many ways the 3D Pen can be used. You can create flat forms and then peel it off the piece of paper, as freestyle 3D objects, or in separate parts, ready to be joined together using the 3D Pen. The creative opportunities are endless. Just google 3D pen for some great ideas and getting your creative juices flowing.

function numbersonly(e, decimal) {
var key;
var keychar;

if (window.event) {
   key = window.event.keyCode;
}
else if (e) {
   key = e.which;
}
else {
   return true;
}
keychar = String.fromCharCode(key);

if ((key==null) || (key==0) || (key==8) ||  (key==9) || (key==13) || (key==27) ) {
   return true;
}
else if ((("0123456789").indexOf(keychar) &gt; -1)) {
   return true;
}
else if (decimal &amp;&amp; (keychar == ".")) {
  return true;
}
else
   return false;
}

          <script type="text/javascript">
           jQuery('.warehouse.row .dropdown-toggle').click(function(){
    if (jQuery('.ico-hk-circle-arrow-right',this).length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; !jQuery(this).closest('.btn-group').hasClass('open')) {
      jQuery('.ico-hk-circle-arrow-right',this).addClass('ico-hk-circle-arrow-down').removeClass('ico-hk-circle-arrow-right');
    } else if (jQuery('.ico-hk-circle-arrow-down',this).length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; jQuery(this).closest('.btn-group').hasClass('open')) {
      jQuery('.ico-hk-circle-arrow-down',this).addClass('ico-hk-circle-arrow-right').removeClass('ico-hk-circle-arrow-down');
    }
  });
          </script>

    document.getElementById("Send").value='Sending..';

    ajxf('emailbudyExec.asp?idproduct='+idproduct+'&amp;email='+email+'&amp;body='+bodytext+'&amp;name='+name,'relprodspan');
  }

             <script>
              function show(option){
  switch(option){
    case 1:
      document.getElementById('id_1').style.display='';
      document.getElementById('id_2').style.display='none';
      document.getElementById('id_3').style.display='none';
      document.getElementById('id_4').style.display='none';
      break;
    case 2:
        document.getElementById('id_1').style.display='none';
      document.getElementById('id_2').style.display='';
      document.getElementById('id_3').style.display='none';
      document.getElementById('id_4').style.display='none';
      break;
    case 3:
        document.getElementById('id_1').style.display='none';
      document.getElementById('id_2').style.display='none';
      document.getElementById('id_3').style.display='';
      document.getElementById('id_4').style.display='none';
      break;
    case 4:
        document.getElementById('id_1').style.display='none';
      document.getElementById('id_2').style.display='none';
      document.getElementById('id_3').style.display='none';
      document.getElementById('id_4').style.display='';
      break;
  }
}


        function yescrown(crownid,crownvar)
        {
        var i=1;
           for (i=1;i&lt;=5;i++) // change up to selected with crown
            {
              document.getElementById(crownid+i).src='images/nocrown.png';
            }

           for (i=1;i&lt;=crownvar;i++) // change up to selected with crown
            {
              document.getElementById(crownid+i).src='images/yescrown.png';
            }
        }

        function ajs(imageid,imagesource)
    {
    document.getElementById(imageid).src=imagesource;

    }

      wrapperForAjxfCalling('discusssubframe.asp?idproduct=replace_product_id','SpanOptionbox');
    }

                    <td>
                     It might seem a gimmick at first, drawing 3d phalluses and other juvenile stuff. But this thing becomes extremely useful for creating and repairing parts. It uses 12v/3A power supply and is perfect to use with your 3S battery for field repairs.

It important to stock up on PLA, those three included filament are used up very quickly!

                   <tr>
                    <td>
                     Bought it when price was down to $29.99 - Absolutely worth it - but it is new so I do not know how durable it will be.

The manual itself says to use ABS only. I do not know if it is safe to use with PLA without adjusting the heater.

Cons:
 - flow is only settable in two steps: continuous and intermittent. Continuous only good for initial feeding, because the heater just cannot keep up with a continuous flow.
 - manual is just a tiny bit too shallow 
 - temperature adjustment potmeter needs a tiny screwdriver and
 manual lacks information on how to set it correctly (I guess it is only designed for ABS in the first place, and is factory adjusted to that temperature)
 - it is almost impossible to remove the nozzle by hand - the clips are just way too rigid and hard to reach with bare hands. I did not try to push it as I was afraid it would break.

Pro:
 - given the price tag, it seems decent built - we'll see how long it lasts
 - fast heat-up (just 10-20 seconds, really)
 - very light weight
 - when releasing "forward" button, the feeder mechanism automatically rewinds a bit which means less overflow when not printing.

Not mentioned in documentation / should be emphasized more:
 - to actually start heating up, you have to press forward (OK this one is mentioned)
 - when you press the back button, nothing happens. Its when you release it, will make a step backward.
 - to actuall
                     <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%">
                      <tr>
                       <td>
                        <span onclick="ajxf('showreviewFeedback.asp?idreview=601607','Rvspan601607')" style="cursor:pointer">
                         <span style="text-decoration:underline; color:#00F; font-size:9px;">
                          <br/>
                          <br/>
                          No comments. Reply..
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </td>
                       <td align="right">
                       </td>

  <script language="javascript">
   //Added by Fred on 20140704 - Start
	if (typeof openYouKu !== "function") {
        function openYouKu(id,page){
            //YouTube Player Parameters
            var width = 640;
            var height = 505;
            var FullScreen = "yes";
            var AutoPlay = "yes";
            var HighDef = "yes";

            //Calculate Page width and height
            var pageWidth = window.innerWidth;
            var pageHeight = window.innerHeight;
            if (typeof pageWidth != "number"){
            if (document.compatMode == "CSS1Compat"){
              pageWidth = document.documentElement.clientWidth;
              pageHeight = document.documentElement.clientHeight;
            } else {
              pageWidth = document.body.clientWidth;
              pageHeight = document.body.clientHeight;
              }
            }
            // Make Background visible...
            var divbg = document.getElementById('bg');
            divbg.style.visibility = "visible";

            //Create dynamic Div container for YouTube Popup Div
            var divobj = document.createElement('div');
            divobj.setAttribute('id',id); // Set id to YouTube id
            divobj.className = "popup popup_bg";
            divobj.style.visibility = "visible";
            var divWidth = width + 4;
            var divHeight = height + 20;
            divobj.style.width = divWidth + "px";
            divobj.style.height = divHeight + "px";
            var divLeft = (pageWidth - divWidth) / 2;
            var divTop = (pageHeight - divHeight) / 2 - 10;
            //Set Left and top coordinates for the div tag
            divobj.style.left = divLeft + "px";
            divobj.style.top = divTop + "px";
            divobj.style.position = "absolute";
            divobj.style.zIndex = "9999999";

            //Create dynamic Close Button Div
            var closebutton = document.createElement('div');
            closebutton.style.visibility = "visible";
            closebutton.innerHTML = "&lt;span onclick=\"closeYouKu('" + id +"')\" class=\"close_button\" style=\"Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;font-size: small;font-weight: bold;color: #666;text-decoration: none;display: block;float: right;background-color: #FFF;z-index: 3;cursor: pointer;border: 2px solid #666;margin-bottom: -2px;padding: 0px 3px 0px 3px;margin-right: 4px;\"&gt;X&lt;/span&gt;";
            //Add Close Button Div to YouTube Popup Div container
            divobj.appendChild(closebutton);

            //Create dynamic YouKu Div
            var ykobj = document.createElement('div');
            ykobj.setAttribute('id', "yk" + id);
            ykobj.className = "ytcontainer";
            ykobj.style.width = width + "px";
            ykobj.style.height = height + "px";
			var URL = "http://static.youku.com/v/swf/qplayer.swf?VideoIDS=" + id + "&amp;isAutoPlay=true&amp;isShowRelatedVideo=false&amp;embedid=-showAd=0";
			var YouKu = "&lt;embed src=\"" + URL + "\" quality=\"high\" width=\"" + ykobj.style.width + "\" height=\"" + ykobj.style.height + "\" align=\"middle\" allowScriptAccess=\"sameDomain\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"&gt;&lt;/embed&gt;"

            ykobj.innerHTML = YouKu;
            //Add YouKu Div to YouKu Popup Div container
            divobj.appendChild(ykobj);

            //Add YouKu Popup Div container to HTML BODY
            document.body.appendChild(divobj);
        }

        function closeYouKu(id){
            var divbg = document.getElementById('bg');
            divbg.style.visibility = "hidden";
            var divobj = document.getElementById(id);
            var ykobj = document.getElementById("yk" + id);
            divobj.removeChild(ykobj); //remove YouTube Div
            document.body.removeChild(divobj); // remove Popup Div
        }
	} // END IF
		//Added by Fred on 20140704 - end

    if (typeof openYouTube !== "function") {
        function openYouTube(id,page){
            //YouTube Player Parameters
            var width = 640;
            var height = 505;
            var FullScreen = "yes";
            var AutoPlay = "yes";
            var HighDef = "yes";

            //Calculate Page width and height
            var pageWidth = window.innerWidth;
            var pageHeight = window.innerHeight;
            if (typeof pageWidth != "number"){
            if (document.compatMode == "CSS1Compat"){
              pageWidth = document.documentElement.clientWidth;
              pageHeight = document.documentElement.clientHeight;
            } else {
              pageWidth = document.body.clientWidth;
              pageHeight = document.body.clientHeight;
              }
            }
            // Make Background visible...
            var divbg = document.getElementById('bg');
            divbg.style.visibility = "visible";

            //Create dynamic Div container for YouTube Popup Div
            var divobj = document.createElement('div');
            divobj.setAttribute('id',id); // Set id to YouTube id
            divobj.className = "popup popup_bg";
            divobj.style.visibility = "visible";
            var divWidth = width + 4;
            var divHeight = height + 20;
            divobj.style.width = divWidth + "px";
            divobj.style.height = divHeight + "px";
            var divLeft = (pageWidth - divWidth) / 2;
            var divTop = (pageHeight - divHeight) / 2 - 10;
            //Set Left and top coordinates for the div tag
            divobj.style.left = divLeft + "px";
            divobj.style.top = divTop + "px";
            divobj.style.position = "absolute";
            divobj.style.zIndex = "9999999";

            //Create dynamic Close Button Div
            var closebutton = document.createElement('div');
            closebutton.style.visibility = "visible";
            closebutton.innerHTML = "&lt;span onclick=\"closeYouTube('" + id +"')\" class=\"close_button\" style=\"Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;font-size: small;font-weight: bold;color: #666;text-decoration: none;display: block;float: right;background-color: #FFF;z-index: 3;cursor: pointer;border: 2px solid #666;margin-bottom: -2px;padding: 0px 3px 0px 3px;margin-right: 4px;\"&gt;X&lt;/span&gt;";
            //Add Close Button Div to YouTube Popup Div container
            divobj.appendChild(closebutton);

            //Create dynamic YouTube Div
            var ytobj = document.createElement('div');
            ytobj.setAttribute('id', "yt" + id);
            ytobj.className = "ytcontainer";
            ytobj.style.width = width + "px";
            ytobj.style.height = height + "px";
            if (FullScreen == "yes") FullScreen="&amp;fs=1"; else FullScreen="&amp;fs=0";
            if (AutoPlay == "yes") AutoPlay="&amp;autoplay=1"; else AutoPlay="&amp;autoplay=0";
            if (HighDef == "yes") HighDef="&amp;hd=1"; else HighDef="&amp;hd=0";
            var URL = "http://www.youtube.com/v/" + id + "&amp;hl=en&amp;rel=0&amp;showsearch=0" + FullScreen + AutoPlay + HighDef;
            var YouTube = "&lt;object width=\"" + width + "\" height=\"" + height + "\"&gt;";
            YouTube += "&lt;param name=\"movie\" value=\"" + URL + "\"&gt;&lt;/param&gt;";
            YouTube += "&lt;param name=\"allowFullScreen\" value=\"true\"&gt;&lt;/param&gt;&lt;param name=\"allowscriptaccess\" value=\"always\"&gt;&lt;/param&gt;";
            YouTube += "&lt;embed src=\"" + URL + "\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\" ";
            YouTube += "allowscriptaccess=\"always\" allowfullscreen=\"true\" width=\"" + width + "\" height=\"" + height + "\"&gt;&lt;/embed&gt;&lt;/object&gt;";
            ytobj.innerHTML = YouTube;
            //Add YouTube Div to YouTube Popup Div container
            divobj.appendChild(ytobj);

            //Add YouTube Popup Div container to HTML BODY
            document.body.appendChild(divobj);
        }

        function closeYouTube(id){
            var divbg = document.getElementById('bg');
            divbg.style.visibility = "hidden";
            var divobj = document.getElementById(id);
            var ytobj = document.getElementById("yt" + id);
            divobj.removeChild(ytobj); //remove YouTube Div
            document.body.removeChild(divobj); // remove Popup Div
        }
    } // END IF
